*Update Note (2026-07-05d, **Phase-0 诊断运行完成 — 金股池 FAIL 生死门 → 弃金股池作策略 universe,量化主线改走宽基**): [run_phase0_diagnostics.py](workspace/research/phase0_golden_pool/run_phase0_diagnostics.py)(预注册:7 ex-approved 因子[注册表方向]+定向复合;67 个 C3 activation 月度调仓期 2020-07..2026-01;h=20d;ln(市值)最近邻孪生对照[不放回];C9 envelope)。**结果**:复合 RankIC/ICIR 池 +0.033/+0.30 vs 市值孪生对照 +0.025/+0.22 vs 宽基 +0.036/**+0.55**(池~177名/对照~174/宽基~4921)。**配对检验(67 期)**:池−对照 mean +0.0082、**t=0.58、p=0.564**(增量无统计支持,胜率 56.7%);池−宽基 t=−0.22(持平)。**判决**:脚本预注册规则名义通过但增量统计为零;**ROADMAP 生死门("打不过 quant-on-broad→弃")FAIL** —— 合并 2026-06-28 母信号判决(金股 EW=市值代理、conviction 反向),两轮证据一致:**券商金股既非信号也非有增量候选池 → 弃作 universe,主线 quant-on-broad**(ROADMAP 下车口,非失败)。**副产品**:7 因子复合宽基 ICIR +0.55(近窗池级旁证,NON-FORMAL);C3 基建(golden_stock_universe PIT 台账/掩码)保留为通用"月度名单型 universe"机器;金股覆盖广度余作 TEXT_REFINERY 候选信号族(analyst-attention/拥挤反指,C16b)选项。[FINDINGS.md](workspace/research/phase0_golden_pool/FINDINGS.md)。NON-FORMAL(窗口叠 spent-OOS 2021+,不铸因子证据)。**下一步 = Phase 1 组合引擎(宽基)**——ROADMAP 真短板:唤醒 portfolio_risk(风险模型+cvxpy 优化器,1×),= capital_allocation_buildout PR1-2。*

*Update Note (2026-07-11, **策略开发方法论 v1.0 建成 + 两轮深度研究判决 + GPT §10 三轮 R1→R2→R3 → APPROVE(设计级,零拒绝)**): 用户诉求——本地系统能验证因子却造不出可部署策略,缺统一方法论。产出 [STRATEGY_DEVELOPMENT_METHODOLOGY_v1.0.md](workspace/research/strategy_development_methodology/STRATEGY_DEVELOPMENT_METHODOLOGY_v1.0.md)(因子-eval v1.4 之上的策略级总纲;commits `f307f3c`→`9f8533e`,分支 `calendar-unfreeze`)。**核心诊断=转移系数(TC)坍缩**:可部署收益来自 信号选择/可交易性 ≫ 成本/换手 > universe > 权重(优化器最后且有条件),经两轮对抗式深研判决核验(Claims 1-5 三票通过;`/deep-research` 工作流,速率限速后分批重跑)+ 平行果仁 #9 实验佐证(MVO 在非微盘书上也没打赢 top-K)。**判决修正三处初判**:Claim1 可交易性是换手-条件性的(慢因子可回收);优化器胜 1/N 的反证被驳(条件变量=特异波动/N/同质性,Platanakis);微盘 10-18% CAGR=未证假设(壳溢价量级被驳)。**北极星被逆转**:先造出一本稳健书,分散组合是后期(1/√ρ≈1.1-1.4× 天花板)。**GPT 跨审**:R1 REVISE(8 硬阻断,含 sealed-OOS 被当优化器选择器 + 引用已过时 E-wave/eps 部署数——两处自审漏)→ R2 REVISE-窄(3 一致性)→ R3 REVISE→APPROVE(仅一处 Part VI parity 措辞)。全部折叠零拒绝,轨迹见同目录 REVIEW_RESPONSE/SELF_REVIEW/DEEP_RESEARCH_ADJUDICATION.md。**方法论=设计级 ground truth;真实策略提升另需实现/测试审查。下一步=BUILD-0**(alpha 标定→轻构造→加权执行→验证台→果仁 parity:造出并证明一本书)。新记忆 [[project_strategy_development_methodology]]/[[feedback_check_concurrent_sessions]]/[[feedback_self_review_before_gpt]]。**本文件今日按 <25k-token 读限拆分:2026-05-31 及更早 + Completed Milestones 移入 [project_state_archive_2026-05_and_earlier.md](project_state_archive_2026-05_and_earlier.md)。***

*Update Note (2026-06-24j, **guorn20 再加权 M3 实现+运行 = holdout 三态裁决 FAIL → 维持等权 (EW)**): 续 24h。引擎 [guorn20_walkforward.py](workspace/scripts/guorn20_walkforward.py) 实现 SHIPPED v5(8 方案 + 封存选择 2023-05-31 + path-correct 配对 stationary block-bootstrap + 三态裁决 + N_eff + max-stat + MLflow)。运行(seed 20260624, 10000 boot, 198 配置/168 deployable, data_hash e956df81, 506s)。**结果: FAIL → 维持 EW**。冻结候选 = two_stage(5 风格组风险平价)/L504/月度/cap15/floor1(pre-holdout 唯一过非劣过滤且 ΔCalmar 中位最高); 但 (1) **family-wise p=0.96**(N_eff=1.86 — 168 配置近共线, 样本内优势落在多重检验噪声内); (2) **holdout(2023-06..2026-06)反转**: ΔCAGR **−3.3pp** / ΔMDD 仅 −0.7pp / ΔCalmar −0.088 / P(ΔCalmar>0)≈0.29 → 三态 **fail**。机制: 风险型加权下调高波微盘成长(A/D), 而 holdout 期高波成长跑赢 → 亏 3.3pp(单一 regime 不可证可部署的活例)。描述性: 样本内风险型普遍压回撤(min_var −9pp MDD)但多数牺牲收益; 27/168 过非劣过滤。**推荐: 保持等权**(N_eff≈2、单一市场/holdout 的诚实默认); two_stage 仅作"偏好更低回撤、可接受更低收益"的取舍变体(未过显著性, 勿当 better-than-EW)。自审修 3 项(turnover tie-break / holdout 仅冻结候选防泄漏 R2-B2 / family_p)。**M4 稳健性余项(子区间/留一族/成本网格/haircut)未跑 — 不能把 fail 翻成 pass, 只强化"维持 EW"**。[GUORN20_FINDINGS.md](workspace/research/capital_allocation_buildout/GUORN20_FINDINGS.md); 实现自审 + GPT 实现审查(§10)待。memory `project_capital_allocation_buildout`。*

*Update Note (2026-06-23b, **果仁 parity RUNG 4 = 全面 holding-level 字段对账 + 模糊因子逆向工程（3 处公式/字段更正 + 1 元发现 + 1 撤回）**): 用户"再爬一级阶梯，将能通过果仁验证的都验证一遍"→"reverse engineer any factors that are ambiguous"。方法=holding-level value parity（rung-2/3 推广）跨 65 本；果仁精确公式取自 [indicator_reference_auto.md](workspace/research/idea_sourcing/guorn/indicator_reference_auto.md)+[guorn_aichat_indicator_defs.md](workspace/research/idea_sourcing/guorn/guorn_aichat_indicator_defs.md)。**财报族逐分匹配**（income+balance+cashflow，超 rung-2 净利润）：GrossProfit%AssetsQ 96.3% w/1%（262k holds）/SalesQGr%PY 95.8%/负债资产率 98.0%/OPCFNPDiff%NP 92.0%。**★ 元发现（可复用）：果仁所有因子按 SIGNAL 日(T-1)显示、非买入日**——4 路独立证（总市值/BP/乖离率/ILLIQ 均偏好 lag1）。**3 处逆向更正**：(1) **BP**=`归属母公司股东权益`(PARENT-only=`$total_hldr_eqy_exc_min_int_q0`)/总市值；原用总权益(inc_min_int)→ 5.9%→**0.66%**（残差=总市值 2 位显示舍入+权益 PIT 边界，两分量均逐分）；(2) **市盈率**=`$pe_ttm` 确认（0.9%），`$pe` 静态错（13.8%）；(3) **ILLIQ(5)** 分子是 **股价振幅 (high-low)/prev_close、非 `|1日涨幅|`**（aichat 公式文本错；描述"每亿元成交额引起的股价振幅"才对），分母 成交额(亿元)=amount(千元)/1e5，avg-of-ratios，signal-lag → 38%→**12.5% within 0.1%**（残差 ~0.86× = 未公开平台子细节）。**数据已验证、残差=重构惯例（非数据错）**：总市值——本地 `$total_mv` 对果仁 `总市值(亿)` 达显示精度（lag1 0.52%/97% w/5%）→ close×shares 逐分。**250日涨幅 & 乖离率(120)**：测试并**证伪 adj-factor 假设（rule #10）**——无 corp-action 子集同样偏（5.4%/8.2%），窗 N=250 尖锐确认最小，比值 复权-不变 → 残差=**N 日回看窗成员计数**（果仁停牌/日历惯例 vs 我 `.shift(N)`/`.rolling(N)`）；符号 95-97%。**撤回**：股价振幅%成交额10日 非逐分（前述声称错）——果仁**显示 0.00**（真值 ~2e-6 在 2 位舍入为零），公式可证正确但对账无意义。**不可复刻**：中性化/壳价值、退市风险/重大违规/未来20日新增流通股、快报。脚本（均 workspace/scripts/，NON-FORMAL）：[_rung4_field_parity.py](workspace/scripts/_rung4_field_parity.py)（BP 已改 exc_min_int）/[_rung4_reverse_engineer.py](workspace/scripts/_rung4_reverse_engineer.py)/[_rung4_decompose.py](workspace/scripts/_rung4_decompose.py)/[_rung4_illiq_bp_final.py](workspace/scripts/_rung4_illiq_bp_final.py)/[_rung4_momentum_diag.py](workspace/scripts/_rung4_momentum_diag.py)。**结论：每个可复刻的果仁数据层已验证（财报逐分；价/市值达显示精度）；非逐分因子是果仁公式/窗惯例细节、非本地数据错。4 阶梯完成。** memory `project_guorn_parity`。*

*Update Note (2026-06-22f, **果仁 parity GPT 跨审 Major-2 已折入 — can_buy 的 IPO no-limit 旁路修复（引擎执行真实度）**): 续 22e 延后的 Major-2（`task_429b338d`）。**问题**：`can_buy` 用 `is_ipo_period(code,date)` 一刀切旁路涨停门——但 `is_ipo_period` 仅按 board+上市天数判"名义 IPO 窗口"，不知**上市日 regime**，故把**注册制改革前主板/创业板首日**（老 **+44%/−36%** 首日涨停限，ASYMMETRIC 但 Tushare 真实发布的 `up_limit`/`down_limit`，如 002728.SZ 2014-07-31 → up_limit 20.16/issue 14.0）误当 no-limit，于是一只锁在 +44% 涨停的 IPO 被"买入"（无卖方）。**修**：新增 `is_true_no_limit_day(code,date,row)` 取代 `can_buy` 的旁路——no-limit 仅当 (1) 已发布 no-limit **SENTINEL**（`up_limit≥99999` ∧ `down_limit≤0.01`，含 BSE 的 99999.99 形态；floor=99999.0 远高于真实最高限价 ~¥3k 又低于 sentinel，永不撞真实限价）**或** (2) 经确认的 **listing-date-regime IPO 窗口**（创业板 list_date≥2020-08-24 / 科创板 首 5 交易日；主板 list_date≥**2023-04-10** 全面注册制 首 5 日；北交所 上市日）；**显式 NOT** 把老主板/改革前创业板 +44% 首日当 no-limit。regime 键于 **list_date 而非交易日**（regime 在上市时固定：2020-08-21 上市的创业板首日仍是老 +44%，即便 ±20% 改革 08-24 生效）。新增常量 `_MAIN_BOARD_REGISTRATION_DATE`/`_NO_LIMIT_UP_SENTINEL_FLOOR`/`_NO_LIMIT_DOWN_SENTINEL_CEIL`。`is_ipo_period` 保留为名义窗口 helper 但**在门中已 DEAD**（docstring 加警告，勿再 wire）。**blast radius 小且无需重跑**：生产路径 row 带 `$up_limit`/`$down_limit`（ENGINE_REQUIRED_FIELDS），真 no-limit 日走 sentinel 分支（is_limit_up 本就 False）→ 行为不变；唯一行为差 = +44% 首日现正确不可买（vs 旧可买）；hist≥20 使其**不入 果仁 parity**，亦**与 22e 的 Major-6 fill-price-aware blast radius 无关**（不改 close/open fill 牛年收益）。**测试**：[test_exchange_limits.py](tests/backtest_engine/test_exchange_limits.py) 新增 `IsTrueNoLimitDayTests`（13 个：3 必需用例〔老主板+44%首日→can_buy False、post-2023主板首5日→True、创业板改革后首5日→True〕+ sentinel 双形态 + STAR/BSE/窗口边界 day6 + pre-reform创业板 + 无feeder保守False），用 `_FakeFeeder`（list_date+count_trading_days business-day 近似）。**47 passed**（含 34 旧）；**全 tests/backtest_engine = 260 passed**（exit 0）。CLAUDE.md §3.3 "Limit detection" + AGENTS.md §2a 同 pass 镜像（§11.2）。**下一步=GPT 5.5 Pro R2 跨审（§10 gate）后 commit/push**（本次是 Major-2 finding 的落地实现，须 re-review 至无 blocker 方为 final）。memory `project_guorn_parity`。*

*Update Note (2026-06-22d, **果仁 parity 阶梯 RUNG 1（sm_纯市值01）= 系统验证通过 + 暴露并修复真实引擎 bug（fill-price-aware 涨跌停门）**): 用户指令=果仁为**可信 benchmark**、本地系统**受测**——复刻真实已部署 guorn 策略以验证本地数据+引擎（系统完整性，非策略再验证；果仁已验证/已部署）。工具 [guorn_parity_rung1_purecap.py](workspace/scripts/guorn_parity_rung1_purecap.py)（D.features 全宇宙 survivorship-free 市值 panel→smallest-市值 schedule，PIT prev-day rank→EventDriven+RankedFallback+果仁成本）+ [guorn_xlsx_ground_truth.py](workspace/scripts/guorn_xlsx_ground_truth.py)。**RUNG 1 抓到两处真问题**：(1) **北证 universe-spec**：果仁 sm_纯市值01 的"全部股票"=**沪深主板+创业板 only**（实证：果仁自身 28,942 持仓行 0 北证/0 科创板，77% 创业板）；本地误含北证→2022 **−56%**（北证 920xxx crash）。修=正向 allow-list `board_of∈{main,chinext}`；附带暴露 `jq_rep_utils.board_of` 把北证 920xxx 误判 bshare（已派 task）。修后 2021-2023 紧贴（2021 +64.7 vs +60.8、2022 +7.2 vs +18.2、2023 +71.1 vs +78.7、换手 ~11x vs 10.3x、MDD −22.6 vs ~−21）。(2) **引擎 fill-price-aware 涨跌停门（真 bug，影响所有 open-fill 回测）**：`is_limit_up`/`is_limit_down`/`can_buy`/`can_sell` 原用 **close** 判涨跌停，故 **open(09:35) fill 误拦每个收在涨停的票**——即便开盘可买。修=加 `price_field`（默认 raw_close=旧行为）、`_execute_orders` 传 fill 列→open fill 用 `raw_open`（只拦开盘一字锁死/调仓时涨停；仅收盘涨停=09:35 可买）；删 RankedFallbackStrategy 昨日涨停预测（改引擎 fill 时判）。**close-based gating on open fills 在每个 open-fill 回测无声少买牛市赢家**（JQ 复刻、E-wave/eps_diffusion 部署门牛年数被低估）。文件 exchange.py/engine.py:718,771/strategies.py；**246/246 tests/backtest_engine 过** + 4 open-vs-close pin + 5 RankedFallback 测试更新到新契约。CLAUDE.md §3.3 + AGENTS.md 镜像。**2015 分解**：+307%（旧 close weekly）→ +396%（open-fix weekly，Δ+89 涨停）→ +462%（open-fix daily，Δ+66 cadence）vs 果仁 +690%。残差 +228 = **construction-rule（非 bug）**：本地等权 rebalance **修剪赢家**（`_emit_rebalance_orders` trim over-allocated），果仁 model-II **持赢家于 5-15% band 且不卖涨停**——牛年放赢家跑值很多。延后的 fill-time substitution(3) **不需要**（全程满仓 cash 0.25%）。**用户指令=复刻须 factor + execution 层完全一致（不接受 weekly vs 果仁 daily 近似）**→ 下一步=建 **faithful model-II daily 策略**（调仓周期1 + buy≤10/sell≥15/hold band + 不卖涨停 + 匹配 filters）后重测。memory `project_guorn_parity`。*

*Update Note (2026-06-22, **平台资深评审（Claude + GPT 双独立）收敛 → 资本配置层 build plan v1（下一阶段路线图）**): 用户请求"以顶级 quant 资深分析师视角深度剖析因子研究机制"。**方法**：4 路并行 codebase 深挖（factor catalog+eval / orchestrator+lifecycle+integrity / portfolio-risk+signal-combination / 执行真实度+容量）+ 综合。**Claude 诊断 + GPT 5.5 Pro 独立评审（经公开 repo）收敛到同一结论**（双独立评审收敛=高置信度）：**价值链倒置**——signal 验证严谨度工业级且部分领先,但把信号转成 PnL 的部分薄。证据：~7 approved 因子/0 部署策略、`strategy_registry` 空、`portfolio_risk` 休眠（`predict_portfolio_risk→0.05`、`fit` no-op、cvxpy `PortfolioOptimizer` 零调用）、风险只有 size+行业中性化、组合=等权 rank、纯多头（中性腿 sim Sharpe 1.46 停着）。**基本法则框**（IR≈IC×√广度×TC）：IC 验得诚实,但广度低（设计如此）+ 转移系数 TC 低（rank→top-K→等权,无优化器）→ 最高 ROI 不是再加因子,是**构建层**。**两处修正双方都认**：(1) **不加杠杆（§7.11）**——期货对冲/中性书是 Sharpe/回撤/分散改善（无杠杆 CAGR ~12-15%、Sharpe 1.4-1.8）,非更高收益（VQ10 价值书 +20.7% 仍是更高 CAGR）；(2) **多重性按 effective trials（族/相关簇）**,非朴素 370×7×4,门是"对集成 IR 的边际贡献"。**强项确认**：研究诚信机制（FrozenSelectionSet 单次 sealed OOS、3-belt PIT walk-forward、ResearchAccessContext、P-GATE、field-status 治理）领先；event-driven 执行真实度（T+1/板块+日期感知涨跌停/停牌退市/公司行动总收益/日期感知印花税）强；部署门两次抓住微盘/流动性驱动的 gross alpha（E-wave、eps_diffusion）；负结果诚实。**build plan v1**（[STRATEGY_LAYER_BUILD_PLAN_v1.md](workspace/research/capital_allocation_buildout/STRATEGY_LAYER_BUILD_PLAN_v1.md),依赖排序）：关键路径 **PR1 风险模型 v1**（行业 one-hot+size+beta+残差波动+流动性+style、EWMA+shrinkage 协方差、idio floor、**A 股 limit-censoring/停牌缺口处理**、接口 fit/predict_covariance/risk_attribution/validate）→ **PR2 优化器接入**（cvxpy MV，gross≤1× 默认，先复刻+改进 VQ10）→ **PR3 StrategyCandidate 生命周期**（镜像 factor lifecycle,扩 `DeploymentFrozenPlan` 成完整 hash-bound book 对象,publish 进空的 strategy_registry,book 也 sealed）；并行 **PR4 容量曲线**（AUM×ADV×impact→capacity stamp,微盘=低容量产品非"坏"）、**PR5 发现端多重性**（effective trials+DSR/PSR+FDR+PBO 接进 promotion 门）、**PR6 期货对冲研究**（先 index proxy,真 IF/IC/IM 账务是独立子系统,排 PR2 后,全程无杠杆）；外加 live 衰减监控/kill 触发。**两条产品线**：liquid 机构线 vs capacity-capped alpha 线（不走同一部署门）。ML 限于 refinement（正则化加权/波动率+成本预测/regime 风险厌恶）,不做 alpha 挖掘（已证过拟合）。北极星里程碑="用已信的因子,产出一个 risk-aware、无杠杆、盖容量章、event-driven 验证、sealed、敢交易的 book"。memory `strategy_knowledge_base` + `project_capital_allocation_buildout`。*

*Update Note (2026-06-21b, **E-wave deployment gate FAILED — 6-core 不可部署；gross OOS Sharpe 经确认为微盘/illiquidity 驱动；E-wave = 已验证证据库、非可部署信号（收口）**): 续 sealed OOS（同日）。6-core 做成**方向对齐等权 z-score 复合**（5 个 held-short 因子做多其低端 + 1 long）、**long-only top-K**、**liquid top-300 by 20d $-vol**、EventDrivenBacktester **1× realistic-China costs**、OOS 2021-01-01→2026-02-26 vs CSI300、[eval_e_wave_v2_deployment.py](workspace/scripts/eval_e_wave_v2_deployment.py)。**FAILED**：top30 realistic **CAGR −3.63% / MDD −52.6% / Sharpe −0.05 / turnover 74%/mo**；top50 −2.89% / −51.4% / −0.02；top30 JQ（乐观成本）−3.85% / −52.9% / −0.06。**负 CAGR、~0 Sharpe、−52% MDD，即便乐观 JQ 成本**（yearly top30 2021-23 −9/−17/−17%、2024-26 +4/+22/+4% = regime 依赖但累计负）。**确认**（非猜测）：gross sealed-OOS LS Sharpe 1.6-5.9 = **微盘/illiquidity 驱动**（全宇宙 decile LS 含不可交易微盘）；限 liquid top-300 + 取 long-only leg + 真成本 → alpha **消失**。同 eps_diffusion（+4.5%/−62%）同陷阱同结局。**裁决：E-wave 6-core = 已验证证据/复刻库，非可部署策略**——mandate fork 落到后者（OOS 过 6/6、deployment gate 失败）。**研究成功而策略失败**：sealed OOS 验证 selection **方法**（外推成立=真）、deployment gate 抓出**不可交易**（微盘绑定=真），二者皆真无矛盾、**资本投入前抓到**（eps_diffusion 教训已内建于流程）。**不重构复合去救**（等权复合在 liquid-300 深度为负 + gross-vs-liquid 缺口 → edge 是 illiquidity-bound；调参对抗已花 OOS=过拟合）。OOS spent、6 留 candidate（未提升）、registry 不变 305。**E-wave 收口**：8 数据章节（E1a-h；E1e 待 cyq_chips）→ 69 候选/~5 族 → 6-core 选择 → 1 次 sealed OOS（6/6）→ deployment gate（FAILED）= 一个方法学健全的复刻练习，产出已验证证据库 + 诚实判定不可部署。docs [E_WAVE_SELECTION_v2.md](workspace/research/cicc_replication/E_WAVE_SELECTION_v2.md)（deployment 段）+ [e_wave_v2_deployment.json](workspace/outputs/e_wave_v2_deployment/e_wave_v2_deployment.json)。与 memory `project_e_wave_selection_mandate`（已更新 STATUS=deployment FAILED）一致。*

不可重摇**；promotion to approved **DEFERRED**（6 留 candidate；registry 不变 305=136 draft/162 candidate/7 approved）。**下一步 = deployment gate**（event-driven、**1×**、realistic costs、**liquid universe top-300 by *Update Note (2026-06-17, **CICC Wave E1b 波动率（图表16）— 算子建+认证 + 36 因子定义/注册 draft（GPT 因子逻辑已 APPROVE）**): E1b 走 算子→因子→注册 链路（matrix+门待续）。**1 个真算子 `sign_conditional_std`**（下行/上行波动率 = sign-matching + limit-excluded 日的**真子集 std**，**非** risk_downvol 的 zero-fill 代理）经 OperatorCertification §10A 在 W∈{20,60,120}×{down,up} 全认证（golden/property/ref-vs-vec/PIT，不烧真值）；构造 ddof=1 sum-of-squares，limit exclusion 读认证字段 `$limit_status`。**实现期数值健壮性修复（3 处，cert 暴露）**：(a) `Greater(var,0)` clamp 子集近相等→tiny-neg variance（sum-of-squares 抵消）；(b) n<2 → NaN 地板**不能**靠 var 的 0/0（rolling-sum 浮点误差使分子 tiny-nonzero→±inf，clamp 把 -inf 误成 0）→ 显式乘 `Ge(n,2)/Ge(n,2)`（n≥2→1、n<2→0/0=NaN）；(c) Qlib `Ge` 返回 **bool**、bool/bool 报错 → `*1.0` 转 float。**`Greater`/`Less` 首用核实**=elementwise max/min（影线用，非自定义算子→manifest 应去 shadow_line）。**36 因子**（13 子类 ×{20,60,120}，`vol_std`≡`risk_vol` 精确去重跳过）入 catalog.py：vol_down/up_std（subset std）、vol_highlow_avg/std（high/low，区别于 risk_range_ratio）、4 影线族 avg/std（Greater/Less，调整因子在比值中抵消）。compute 实测全 sane（0 负、子集 std < 全 vol、shadow∈[0,~0.02]）、**vol_down_std vs risk_downvol corr 0.894（<1.0 = 忠实子集 std 确异于代理）**、PIT-safe。sync_catalog 入注册表 draft：registry **224→260**（156 draft / 97 candidate / 7 approved）。测试 operator-expressions+catalog-parity+PIT 107 过。driver [certify_e1b_operators.py](workspace/scripts/certify_e1b_operators.py)；spec [E1b_factor_logic.md](workspace/research/cicc_replication/E1b_factor_logic.md)（GPT B1-B4 已折入 APPROVE）。**下一步：v2 manifest 修正（去 shadow_line、链 36 catalog_factor_id）→ 7域矩阵 → P-GATE → IS 门**。resolve-but-label，无提升。*

*Update Note (2026-06-17, **新派生 PIT-safe 字段 `$limit_status` 物化 + 注册(涨跌停日 exclusion 的单一认证源)**): E1b GPT 审 B2 指出"剔除涨跌停日须 raw/adjusted 基准安全";用户选"现在就建物化 PIT-safe 字段,把一切建在正确基准上,而非日后返工"(而非我建议的 inline 共享常量)。**实现**:`$limit_status` = 三态涨跌停标志（+1 close≥up_limit / −1 close≤down_limit / 0 正常 / NaN 停牌或无限价），由 provider build 从**原始** `$close` vs **原始** `$up_limit`/`$down_limit` 计算（[pit_backend.py](src/data_infra/pit_backend.py) 新增模块级纯函数 `compute_limit_status` + 方法 `_materialize_derived_limit_status`，接在 daily-dataset 循环后；半 fen 容差，float32-robust）。**基准安全 by construction**（三输入皆原始同日，绝不混调整价 vs 原始限价 = GPT 标的最可能静默 bug）。**回填**(无须全量重建)：[scripts/backfill_limit_status.py](scripts/backfill_limit_status.py)（dry-run 默认）读各 symbol 已写的 close/up_limit/down_limit bin（validator 保证 close-aligned）写 limit_status.day.bin；**实跑 5748 symbol、0 misaligned、0 越域值、涨跌停率 2.69%**（up 250929 / down 133585 / normal 13.9M，up>down 合 A 股史）。**D.features 验证定义 100% 成立**（每 +1 行 close≥up_limit、每 −1 行 close≤down_limit、0 正常行处于限价），域 {−1,0,1,NaN}。**注册**（formal 数据门）：[field_status.yaml](config/field_registry/field_status.yaml) `limit_status: approved` + [approval YAML](config/field_registry/approvals/2026-06-17_limit_status_derived_to_approved.yaml)（binding `indicators_fields_20260609`/`frozen_20260227_system_build`）+ append-only log；`resolve_field($limit_status,*)` → status_id=approved/allowed=True。**同日 close 可知**（用 close，区别于 session-open 的 $up_limit/$down_limit）→ 预测因子须 Ref(...,1)。**单一认证源**供整个价量 wave 的涨跌停 exclusion（E1b 上/下行波动、mmt_off_limit、下游批次），未来 build 经接好的物化步自动维护。测试:field_registry+approval_evidence 88 过、pit_backend+provider_boundary 32 过。**下一步:E1b `sign_conditional_std` 消费 `$limit_status`**。（本 commit 另携并发会话遗留的 report_rc field-governance discharge 补齐——见 2026-06-15 entry，pre-existing 未提交，随同提交以免治理半提交。）*

*Update Note (2026-06-17, **残差控制域 BUG 修复 + 矩阵两层 decoupling 重建 + 门控 live import + D4a/P-GATE 决策-delta（整弧闭环；GPT 5.5 Pro 全程跨审 GO）**): 跨 2026-06-15→17 的完整一弧，本条为用户钦定的"单条 coherent 记录"。**(1) BUG（V4 字节相等证伪 → 真 eval-correctness 缺陷，非数据）**:`_evaluate_batch` 装配 `processed = {**resident_processed, **batch_processed}` 把**全市场 winsorize 的 resident 控制项**（未掩码 seed）与**子universe 掩码 winsorize 的 batch 控制项**混用；winsorization 非仿射 → 控制项 scope 取决于 eval-batch 成员 → 残差**批序相关**（batch-0 resident 因子拿掩码控制、非 resident 拿全市场）。受控实验定性:seed==fresh 位级相同（排除数据）；单因子 vs 批 显批依赖；全市场 vs 掩码控制精确复现 −0.014566 vs −0.016068。**(2) FIX（GPT 钦定 Barra/Axioma 标准 transform-then-mask）**:候选 AND 控制项都在**固定宽 ESTU**（`ESTU_STYLE_V1`=全panel）winsorize+z-score，**再**掩码到 eval universe，**之后**才做逐日 OLS 残差 + IC；`residual_preprocess_scope` 升为 `EvalMethodology` 的 hashed 旋钮（进 `layer1_methodology_hash` → 强制重建）。univ_all 处 broad==eval → 修复是结构性 no-op（所以 univ_all 因子本就未受影响）。`residual_ic_vs_controls(..., eval_mask, preprocess_scope)`、`_mask_to_eval_universe`（小缺口 fillna(False)、>1% gross-mismatch raise）。**(3) 两层 decoupling 架构**:Layer-1 = reference-INVARIANT 矩阵（含 `resid_ic_vs_style_controls_v1` 风格残差，键 `layer1_methodology_hash`）= **选因子基准**；Layer-2 = `resid_ic_vs_approved_{stable,current}`（marginal-vs-book，reference-DEPENDENT）= **仅描述**，落 append-only `Layer2ResidualStore`。**用户决定（2026-06-15）**:按**风格残差**（冻结 14-因子机构 `STYLE_CONTROLS_V1`）选因子，approved-book 残差降级描述。**已验证:无任何 code 对 `resid_ic_vs_approved` 做 pass/fail/选择决策**（仅 dashboard 显示 + evidence *Update Note (2026-06-14, **P-OP OperatorCertification 骨架落地 — E1 价量~135 因子的硬前置**): 路线图 canary 后的下一步(§10A)。新模块 [operator_certification.py](src/alpha_research/factor_library/operator_certification.py)(与 operators.py 同包,parquet+file_lock):**(1) 状态解析** `resolve_operator_status`——全四类测试过=certified / 任一显式 False=blocked(错算子硬封) / 缺测=experimental。**(2) 通用认证 harness** `run_certification` 四类测试——`golden_panel`(手算小例)/ `property_based`(退化/尺度不变式)/ `reference_vs_vectorized_random`(慢速参考 vs 生产 vectorized 随机面板对拍=核心正确性钉)/ `pit_alignment`(因果性);**关键 §10A/R2-B3 解耦:NO truth_parity——认证只证算子语义/对齐/PIT,绝不看真值表故不烧 OOS**。**(3) OperatorCertStore**——status_of 对无记录因子返回 `blocked`(fail-closed)。**(4) 实战样例** [certify_operators.py](workspace/scripts/certify_operators.py):`amplitude_conditional_sum`(CICC mmt_range 建块=高振幅日滚动收益和)四测全过 → certified 持久化。**(5) 接门**:`_cohort_ceiling` 的 `has_uncertified_operator` 现查 cert store(built-in `add_composites` OR cert-store certified;handler 失败 fail-closed=none certified→未认证算子 block)。**自查发现并修了 PIT 测试缺陷**:原 `safe=len-perturb-window` 会让"小于窗口的 1 步前视"漏网;改为"扰动未来行 [k:],断言 [:k] 输出不变(因果算子 output[<k] 只依赖 input[<k])",可捕获任意前视(测试实证 shift(-1) 算子被 pit+reference 双双拦下)。测试 [test_operator_certification.py](tests/alpha_research/test_operator_certification.py) 9 + 全套 77 过。**E1 价量复刻现可推进**:每新算子走 harness 认证→certified→其因子方可进 formal IS(未认证=dev-evidence)。骨架不要求一次认证所有算子(§12.1)。*

*Update Note (2026-06-14, **CICC Rev5 路线图开工 — 治理骨架落库(item 1/3,GPT 三轮 APPROVE 的"可开工最小前置集")**): 用户"开始下一步"→ 实装 Rev5 Round-3 钦定的实现起点第一项。新模块 [replication_governance.py](src/alpha_research/factor_registry/replication_governance.py)(与 domain_claims.py 同包同约定:parquet+file_lock,_PROJECT_ROOT parents[3]):**(1) 确定性 status_ceiling lattice**(§12.4)——`resolve_status_ceiling` 由严到松单遍走(blocked→dev_evidence_only→evidence_only→candidate_ceiling→eligible_for_oos→eligible_for_approved),最严 cap 胜出,物化**单一** ceiling + reason codes(cap=须移除 / gate=须获取,两类分开);**§11.1b 硬编码**:`orientation_undetermined` 等弱信号 NON_CEILING_FLAGS 作 cap 传入即 fail-closed(强制路由到 uncomputable_metrics,弱信号≠不合格)。**(2) CohortManifest**(§9.1)——冻结 YAML + 内容寻址 manifest_sha(改动即可检测),`load_cohort_manifest` 校验声明 sha;**5 层 denominator**(§9.2)前 3 层(source/daily_replicability/formalization_candidate)冻结、后 2 层(exact_oos_eligible/sealed_attempt)下游追踪;`cohort_pass_rate` 拒绝裸分数(必带三分母,防 p-hacking 挑分母)。**(3) compute_oos_quarantine_start**(§9.3)——`max(system_oos_start, truth_label_end+horizon+embargo)`,交易日历注入式(无注入则保守日历日回退并标 approximate)。**(4) ReplicationGovernanceRecord store**(§12.3)——一条 per-(cohort,factor,claim) 记录替 6 套账,upsert 时由 resolver 定 ceiling(调用方不能自指派),幂等。**冻结清单** [config/replication/cicc_fundamental_cohort_v1.yaml](config/replication/cicc_fundamental_cohort_v1.yaml):中金基本面手册 source=112(105+7复合,权威表头)、daily_replicability=95(可行性汇总✅+⚠估计,带 provenance)、formalization_candidate=46(枚举 D5×18+D-COMP×8+D4a×10+D4b×2+D6×8,与行数一致);truth_label_end=2022-12-31(Phase-D 观察 2010-2022→OOS 隔离驱动);全行 oos_eligibility=short_window/pending(诚实:看了真值表→新窗短,§9.4)。测试 [test_replication_governance.py](tests/alpha_research/test_replication_governance.py) 29 过(lattice 每档+最严胜出+§11.1b fail-closed / manifest 冻结+sha 篡改检测 / OOS 隔离算术 / store 幂等)。**状态:骨架落库,尚未接入门**(enforcement = item 2 P-GATE/F3,下一步:FactorDomainClaim/TaintLedger 接门 + 生产 resolver block evidence-only 域 + availability_audit;之后 D-COMP/D4a 作首批 canary)。骨架是纯治理记账,自身不裁决、不读行情(日历注入)。*

*Update Note (2026-06-14, **dashboard "数据/定义漂移" 误报根因 + 87 因子按 2010-2020 新窗重签(用户门批)**): 用户问"为何大量因子 formal ICIR 旁出现 ⚠ 人签与自动同口径分歧"。**根因(已证实,非猜测)**:那个 canary 比的是 |人签留出ICIR − 自动留出ICIR|,设计前提"同引擎→分歧=数据/定义漂移"只在同 IS 窗才成立;但人签证据是旧 2014-2020 窗(phase6 候选闸,无 methodology_hash)、自动全量是我 06-13 切到的新 2010-2020 窗 → 跨窗差异是换窗预期,非漂移。**铁证**:risk_vol_5d 三行——人签 −0.5104(旧窗)/06-10 refresh −0.5104(旧窗,逐位复现人签,drift=0)/06-13 auto −0.4013(新窗);因子定义与数据全程未变,只窗口变。90/94 因子全被误标。**修复(两段)**:(1) 比较键从 methodology_hash 改为 **IS 窗相等**(候选闸结构上不产 methodology_hash,窗是唯一可靠键)——[content.py](src/dashboard/content.py) 读 unified_metrics_json 的 effective_start/end;同窗→真 drift(⚠ if>0.005)、异窗→↻ 待重签、异窗且新窗 auto 不过候选闸→▼ 宽窗减弱。(2) **重签**:[record_lifecycle_evidence](src/alpha_research/factor_registry/store.py) 增窗+universe_id 落痕(additive);驱动 [resign_candidates_2010_2020.py](workspace/scripts/resign_candidates_2010_2020.py) 用矩阵已算的新窗 run_is_walk_forward(factor_origin=a_priori,与候选闸逐位一致)数复签。**用户 AskUserQuestion 显式门批(=gate-review approved)**:95 签字集在新 2010-2020 窗对候选闸(|ICIR|≥0.10∧符号一致≥0.70)再验证 → **87 过 → 重签(formal_evidence_eligible=True,attached=87,0 定义漂移,store.save 已持久化)**;**8 减弱(comp_relative_strength/mom_idio_20d/qual_accruals/rev_min_return_20d/risk_downvol_20d/val_cftp/val_sp/val_sp_ttm,多为价值类符号一致<0.70 跨 2010-13 政权)→ 维持 candidate(resolve-but-label,用户选"只标不降),标 ▼ 待人工复核**——真实再验证发现非错误。dashboard 实测:87 同窗 ✓(drift=0,头条=新窗数)/0 误报 ⚠/8 个 ▼;指标说明加 ⚠/↻/▼ 三标解释。测试:test_factor_registry+dashboard_boundaries 35 过、test_factor_lifecycle_steps 17 过。Provenance:[resign_provenance.json](workspace/research/factor_resign_2010_2020/resign_provenance.json)(含门批授权文本+87 重签+8 旗标)。**教训:换 IS 窗后人签证据即陈旧,canary 比较键必须是同窗;跨窗"漂移"是误报。***

*Update Note (2026-06-10, **北向掩码 vs 未掩码 unified-eval evidence-only 对照（用户指令）+ 全量 185 unified-eval 完成**): 全量 unified_eval 185/185 跑完（supervisor attempt-1 即成功，18:33 exit 0；导入流程仍待办）。随后按用户指令做掩码对照：给 canonical 驱动 [unified_eval_full_run.py](workspace/scripts/unified_eval_full_run.py) 加 `--factors`/`--outdir` 子集模式（`--factors` 强制要求 `--outdir`，子集跑永不混入生产 results.jsonl），在独立目录以**同一新方法学哈希 `6598094c`**（9-approved 参照集，commit d2c2ef3）重评 7 个北向形式 + 本批另 3 因子。**直接配对裁决（zero-densification 定论）**：`north_hold_change_20d` 未掩码 → `_cov` 掩码：中性化 RankICIR **0.097→0.329（3.4×）**、中性化 HAC-t 0.83（不显著）→**2.79**、tie_rate 0.287→0.005、长腿 IR (CSI500) 0.12→1.80；raw heldout 不变（0.61→0.60）——证实 `` 零填充的 ~50% 零平局质量在吸收规模/行业回归、专杀**中性化**信号（这就是未掩码 catalog 形式 raw 看着好、neut 全废的机制）。`north_hold_change_60d_cov` 更强（neut 0.458/HAC-t 3.46、40d 衰减 ICIR 反升至 0.70）。**结论（纯证据、零注册动作）**：within-coverage 是正确构造，但救不了维度——sealed-OOS 已证掩码形式 2021-2026 同样符号翻转（更好的测量，方向已反转的信号）。**常设教训：未来任何 hk_hold 因子必须 mask 到 ratio>0；5 个未掩码 catalog draft 维持原状**（底层信号已 OOS 失败，重构无意义）。附录：`earn_sue_ni_mcap` 本批最强中性化（0.562/HAC-t 6.3）但 OOS LS 不过 bar；approved 的 `earn_sue_ni_assets` 是唯一干净 monotonic_up；`alpha_chip_cgo_smooth_20d` 残差正交性最佳（0.058）+年换手 0.97 的漂亮 IS 行 ×OOS 已死——unified Tier-1 质量与 OOS 存活是两根轴。对照全文：[D1_D4_SCREEN_RESULTS.md](workspace/research/idea_sourcing/knowledge/D1_D4_SCREEN_RESULTS.md)；数据 `workspace/outputs/unified_eval_north_cov_compare/`。*

*Update Note (2026-06-10, **arXiv 知识框架：把"论文火管"做成"价值排序+方向聚类"的研究方向入流（用户："进一步挖掘 arxiv 论文中的因子；构建一套知识框架，从 arxiv 获取最有价值的论文并找到研究方向"）**): 既有 `fetch_arxiv_qfin.py` 只是"取最新 N 篇 q-fin 落地存储就停"——是火管不是框架。新建**四层知识框架**（`workspace/research/idea_sourcing/knowledge/` + `enrich/`，Class-D 研究工具，不碰 PIT/Qlib/registry，论文=假设源永不为证据）：**核心价值定义**——一篇论文对本系统的价值 ≈ `P(产出一个新的、正交的、可部署的 A 股因子)`，而非引用数/新近度；该概率只在论文同时(a)讲横截面股票收益(b)能用我们有的数据算(c)落在我们尚未饱和的维度时才高。**层0 取数**：`fetch_arxiv_qfin.py` 加 `--query-pack frontier`——按前沿维度的 ~45 个主题短语做**相关性收割**（AND-of-词，非精确短语；relevance 排序），类目扩到 `q-fin.*+cs.LG+econ.EM+stat.ML`，并入去重存储（旧 newest-N 模式保留为默认）。**层1 知识骨干** [taxonomy.py](workspace/research/idea_sourcing/knowledge/taxonomy.py)：我们的数据清单(16 有/12 无能力)+ 研究维度分类法(每维标**我们的饱和状态**)+ 打分词典；饱和图源自 OSAP 教训(12 移植→1 候选→0 可部署)——价/量/质/波动/规模/流动性 **SATURATED**，分析师·盈利事件·知情资金流·持股·行为筹码 = **FRONTIER_OPEN**(数据刚批准但几乎没挖)，文本/微结构/期权/供应链 = **FRONTIER_BLOCKED**(缺数据)。**层2 打分** [score_papers.py](workspace/research/idea_sourcing/knowledge/score_papers.py)：确定性离线(可复现)，`composite = relevance_gate × Σ wᵢ·子分(维度·实证·新近·影响·中国)`；relevance_gate 对加密/外汇/债券**硬否决**封顶；两套预设 frontier(默认,找新方向)/established(影响力主导,找经典)。**层3 方向图** [build_research_map.py](workspace/research/idea_sourcing/knowledge/build_research_map.py)：按分类法聚类→`RESEARCH_DIRECTIONS.md`(脚手架)+顶部可部署前沿论文的 draft 预注册 stub。**层4 影响信号** [enrich_openalex.py](workspace/research/idea_sourcing/enrich/enrich_openalex.py)：OpenAlex 引用/期刊(keyless polite pool；对 2026 预印本天然稀疏,frontier 预设权重仅 0.12 故鲁棒；修了标题标点致 400 的 bug + 不重试 400)。**首跑(671 篇主题语料,从 80→671)产出 4 个 Tier-1 可即建前沿方向**([TOP_DIRECTIONS.md](workspace/research/idea_sourcing/knowledge/TOP_DIRECTIONS.md))：**D1 资本利得悬置(CGO)/处置效应 自 `cyq_perf`**(⭐ 首选——源论文直接在 A 股测过 1995-2024、行为维度、与 182 因子簿正交、cyq_perf 已批准但零因子用过；`behav_cgo=(Ref($close,1)−Ref($cyq_perf__weight_avg,1))/Ref($cyq_perf__weight_avg,1)`)、**D2 知情资金流 自 `moneyflow`**(大/超大单净额；字段文档自己给了配方 `(buy_lg+elg−sell_lg+elg)/turnover`)、**D3 盈利惊奇/PEAD**(statements+forecast/express；与 eps_diffusion 相邻但不同信号)、**D4 北向资金 自 `hk_hold`**；外加方法学升级(empirical-Bayes 因子筛选 抗因子动物园多重检验)与受阻数据采集目标(财报电话会文本=最大受阻前沿、供应链图、基金持仓)。全套设计文档 [KNOWLEDGE_FRAMEWORK.md](workspace/research/idea_sourcing/knowledge/KNOWLEDGE_FRAMEWORK.md)。守卫不变：方向→因子仍须走 sandbox→**边际正交检验 vs 簿**(房规[[reference_factor_selection_marginal_not_icir]])→factor_lifecycle→sealed-OOS；框架只抬高"找到真方向"的概率，不降任何闸。下一步:实建 D1(CGO) 跑 eps_diffusion 同款 gauntlet。*

*Update Note (2026-06-10, **统一因子评估标准（设计+2轮 GPT 跨审+P0a 正确性核心落地）—— 起因：仪表盘"评级"列对 8 个 approved 因子显示"—"**): 用户问为何 approved 因子无评级/ICIR。根因：仪表盘 [content.py:306-307](src/dashboard/content.py#L306) 的评级/5d-RankICIR 列**只读 `run_type='screening'`（批量筛选）证据**，而 walk-forward+sealed-OOS 晋升的因子从未跑过该 screening → grade 空 → "—"（同列混了 5d 字母评级 vs 20d walk-forward ICIR 两套不可比口径）。决定建**一套对全 185 因子同口径、IS-only、零 OOS 消耗、evidence-only（永不改注册状态）的统一标准**。**三层设计**（[unified_eval_standard.md](workspace/research/factor_expansion/unified_eval_standard.md)）：Tier1 内在（留出 RankICIR+符号一致+均值IC+IC命中+单调形状+衰减+换手+覆盖+中性化IC+多头腿净成本超额）、Tier2 边际正交（残差IC vs approved参照集，leave-one-out + vs 风格控制集；**等权增量ICIR 实测后否决**——混淆等权稀释与单体强度，与"按边际选因子"原则相反）、Tier3 稀疏金牌（仅真花过 sealed-OOS）。**7 因子验证**（`unified_eval_probe.py`/`unified_eval_verify2.py`，缓存面板）：留出 ICIR+符号一致**逐位复现已存证据**；边际残差 IC 印证 [[reference_factor_selection_marginal_not_icir]]（liq_vol_cv 单体|ICIR|0.70 但正交后仅留 37% 冗余 vs gross_profitability 单体 0.138 留 109% 纯增量）；单调诊断自动抓出 eps_diffusion 的 `top_reversal`（体部 Q1–Q4 单调、顶桶反转）——独立印证其"真 alpha 非可部署 long-only"。**A股做空约束**：组合 LS 是纸面数（融券限标的池、无股指期货数据），可部署=多头腿净成本超额 vs 基准。**两轮 GPT 跨审**：Rev2（首轮）+ **Rev3（GPT 5.5 Pro 云端读实现代码）抓到真问题且经我逐一核实属实**：(1) `bootstrap_sharpe_ci` 是 IID Sharpe 非 block/非 IC → overlap-t **未实现**（statsmodels 未装）；(2) `compute_ic_decay` 内部 `price(t+h)/price(t)-1` **无 is_end 守卫** → h=40 泄漏；(3) 注册表 `expected_direction` 是 `_expected_direction(heldout)` **观测得来** → 用它定向单调=循环；(4) 我的能力矩阵系统性混淆"原语存在 vs 有经测试的生产 helper"。**P0a/P0b/P0c 正确性+统计核心已落地+测试**：新增 [src/alpha_research/factor_eval/unified_eval.py](src/alpha_research/factor_eval/unified_eval.py)——**P0a**：`leak_safe_decay_ic_vector`（每 horizon 独立 `build_is_windowed_panel` 裁剪，h=40 自动丢实现日越界的尾日）、`resolve_orientation`（经济先验优先，否则**训练折符号**，绝不读观测的注册表方向）、`classify_quantile_shape`（提为模块函数）；**P0b**：`hac_mean_tstat`（内部 Bartlett-kernel Newey-West HAC，免 statsmodels；对重叠标签的虚高 IID-t 做修正——测试证正自相关序列 HAC-SE>IID-SE）+ `moving_block_bootstrap_mean_ci`（日级序列移动块 bootstrap，非 IID，确定性）；**P0c**：`one_way_turnover`（真单向 `|Δ|/(|A|+|prev|)×252/rebal` + tie-rate + 上下桶分开）+ `long_leg_excess_ir`（多头腿等权 top-q 净成本超额 vs 基准 IR——A股可部署口径，组合 LS 不可部署）。[tests/alpha_research/test_unified_eval.py](tests/alpha_research/test_unified_eval.py)（含 train 正/full 负仍取 train 的非循环证明、衰减零越界保证、HAC>IID、换手静态≈0/轮动高、多头腿正超额）。**round-2 GPT 5.5 Pro 实现审查(读 GitHub 真实代码逐函数)→ 确认核心修复正确,抓到几个真实小问题,逐一核实后修(本批)**：①换手在桶大小漂移时是 membership-churn 非真换手(GPT 100/200 例:真等权单向 0.5 vs symdiff 0.333)→ 改 `0.5·Σ|Δw|`；②`long_leg_excess_ir` 缺基准日 excess 变 NaN 被丢但 prev_top 仍推进 → 改 **fail-closed(raise)**；③`resolve_orientation` 弱因子任意微小均值→±1 → 加 **HAC|t|<1 弱信号守卫→undetermined + orientation_valid**(并修常量序列 *Update Note (2026-06-10, **看板故事线补"全貌"：每假设加 IS-vs-OOS 实测表现面板 + 自动制度警示（用户："hypothesis 故事线不完整，需要每次 research 的全貌"）**): 上一版故事线只显示"闸的判定"（criteria 药丸），不显示**实测回测表现**。现 [`governance.py`](src/dashboard/governance.py) 从 run 工件实读每个 gate 阶段的真实表现——`validation_event_backtest_{is,oos}/event_driven_summary.json`（CAGR/总收益/基准/超额/Sharpe/MDD/IR/Beta/Alpha/胜率/波动/天数，中文带括号英文键按英文尾精确匹配避免 Sharpe vs Excess-Sharpe 混淆）+ `validation_diagnostics_*/metrics.json`（年化换手 + rank_icir）；fail-soft，run_dir 不在则按 `workspace/` 尾在 PROJECT_ROOT 下重根。[`render.py`](src/dashboard/render.py) `_metrics_panel` 在卡里加 **📊 实测表现**段——IS 全样本 vs OOS 封存窗**同口径并排表**（年化 CAGR/Sharpe/最大回撤(>35% 标红)/IR/Beta/换手/胜率/同期基准/交易天数；只列可比的年化/比率指标 + benchmark+天数给 horizon 语境，避开累计收益跨期误比）。**自动制度警示**：OOS Sharpe>1.8×IS 且 IS-MDD>35% → 卡头 **⚠制度依赖** 徽章 + 警示句（可文本筛"制度依赖"）。落点正是上条 lxr_005 审查：卡上现一眼看到 IS 20.5%/Sh0.75/**MDD49.3%(红)** vs OOS 107.7%/Sh2.96/MDD12.5%，同期基准 IS49.5%(2676日) vs OOS51.2%(277日)=牛市指纹——"OOS 太好看"被 IS 现实当场打脸。覆盖：11 假设有 IS 面板（全家 IS-MDD 46-58% 全标红），仅 lxr_005 有完整 IS+OOS（故唯一触发制度警示）；**副发现 lxr_004 也 approved 但只有 is_only gate（无 OOS 跑），其 OOS 列全"–" → 看板现暴露"哪些 approved 只有 IS 证据、没跑封存 OOS"**。DOM 实测 9 行表/红 MDD/警示文案/段序 🎯📊🪜🏁 正确，无 console error；构建 865KB。*

*Update Note (2026-06-10, **看板研究层加 filter + 审查 `hyp_20260527_lxr_005` 的 100% OOS CAGR（用户问"收益为何这么高"）→ 结论：真实算术但作为可部署预期具误导性，是"制度/年化/良性窗口"三重放大，非泄漏**): 两件事。**(1) 研究层筛选**：三子页各加 filterbar（治理页=状态药丸 approved/rejected/registered + 文本搜 假设id/thesis/因子/profile；线程页/里程碑页=文本），复用因子层 `applyFilter`（`data-scope`/`data-row`/`.fhide`）；DOM 实测 18 卡→approved 2、文本 lxr→6、线程 idea→1，无 console error。**(2) lxr_005 审查（重要 finding）**：用户问这个 approved 假设 OOS 为何 CAGR 100.76%/Sharpe 2.96/MDD −12.45%。直读 run_dir `workspace/outputs/hypothesis_validation/lxr_v5_20260527_112442` 的 IS/OOS diagnostics+event_driven_summary+report.csv+prescription。**确凿结论（无对冲）**：①**基准本身暴涨**——OOS 窗（2025-01-02→2026-02-27，277 日）CSI500(000905.SH) 自身 **+51.2%**（引擎 bench 日收益复利实测 51.2%，与 summary 一致），策略 beta 0.78 → ~+40pp 是纯市场 beta（"924"刺激+2025 小盘 melt-up 历史性牛市）。②**"107% CAGR" 是单个 13.5 月牛窗年化、非可持续率**——总收益 +123.3%/13.5 月年化成 107%；**同策略 IS(2014-2024, 11y) 复利仅 20.5% CAGR**（5× 低）。③**12% 的 OOS 回撤掩盖真实 49% 回撤风险**——同一本子 IS MDD **49.3%**（2015 崩盘→2018 熊）/Sharpe **0.74**；2025 OOS 窗无持续熊（仅 4 月初 3 日关税跌 −12%）故 Sharpe 印成 2.96。④**设计正好压中制度**：小盘 tilt(size lower-better)+资金流+价值+低流动性波动+反转 = 拥挤的小盘动量/资金流交易，最大化吃 2025 小盘潮；IS-MDD-49% / OOS-MDD-12% 不对称即指纹。**非泄漏**：universe 生存者安全（all_market PIT 含退市、≥¥1bn、上市≥250 日）、时间分割干净（IS≤2024-12-31 / OOS=冻结日历最后 14 月真实前向窗）、因子走 sealed windowed-features。（diagnostics 的 OOS rank_ic 与 IS 字节相同 0.1488417136460393 = stub 未重算 OOS IC 的瑕疵，但不影响 event-driven 回报，IS 20% vs OOS 107% 确实不同。）**审批本身是 override**——IS 硬闸 MDD 0.50/turnover 7.3 被记录在案地放行（正是看板"⚠超1硬闸"标记）。**与 [[strategy_v2_val_heavy_invalidated]]/[[research_long_only_50cagr]]/eps_diffusion 同一课**：过闸/approved ≠ 可部署在该收益率；可部署真相是 through-cycle IS（~20% CAGR / Sharpe 0.74 / ~49% MDD / 高换手），100% 是制度+年化+良性窗三重放大的产物。脚本：直读上述 run 工件（未改任何研究数据）。*

*Update Note (2026-06-10, **看板正式研究治理：从"摊平5表"重构为"每假设一条故事线"（用户反馈：缺一目了然的"测什么/每步证实了什么/最终结论"）**): 用户指出昨天的治理页只是把所有研究的每一步按类型摊平罗列（① 假设表 ② run 表 ③ 裁决 ④ 封存 ⑤ 状态变迁），看不出单个 hypothesis 在测什么、每步证实了什么、最终实现了什么。**重构 [`governance.py`](src/dashboard/governance.py)+[`render.py`](src/dashboard/render.py)**：把 ① 改成**按假设切的故事线卡**（18 张，可展开）——每卡三段：**🎯 测试什么**（解析 registration 的 `hypothesis_json`：thesis + mechanism + 预期效应 `expected_effect`（statistic/点估/CI/horizon/方向）+ **成功标准 `success_criteria`**（预先承诺的闸：rank_icir≥/deflated_sharpe≥/MDD≤/turnover≤/corr≤）+ 因子 + universe/benchmark/rebalance）；**🪜 每一步证实了什么**（时间线：预注册→各 gate_decision，每个 gate 把 `criteria_results_json` 渲成逐条 pass/fail 药丸 `metric actual comp threshold ✓/✗`，并附 `decision_reason`）；**🏁 最终结论**（终态 + 理由）。**三态判定**（修了一个会误导的点）：criteria 的 `passed` 是 True/False/None → ✓通过(绿)/✗硬性未过(红, is_hard)/✗软性未达(琥珀)/–未计算(灰, 如 `monotonicity_pvalue=None`)；折叠摘要一行 `thesis… → 终态（末闸 rank_icir 值）`。**核心治理事实被显式暴露**：3 个 approved 假设其实是**带硬闸未过被记录在案地批准**（如 `hyp_20260527_lxr_005`：is_only 5/8 通过含 MDD 0.50>0.35、turnover 7.3>4.0 两条硬闸未过，oos_test 又 1 条 turnover 未过，`decision_reason` 写明 override 理由）→ 折叠摘要加红色 **⚠超N硬闸** 标记，一眼可见"不是干净过闸"。② ③ ④ ⑤ 明细表折叠进"② 原始治理记录"可展开块（保留可排序）。顶部加药丸图例。原始数据全部真实（DOM eval 实测：18 卡、三段齐全、40 时间线步、66 绿+53 红+30 灰药丸、lxr_005 故事线正确、override 标记 3 个、na 灰 rgb(110,118,129)、无 console error）。构建 0.8s。*

*Update Note (2026-06-10, **看板翻译补译做成"会话内一键"`/backfill-translations`；headless `claude -p` 自动化此机不可行（实测 401，记录以免重查）**): 用户想把"新因子缺中英文描述"的补译自动化、且无 Anthropic API key（只能走 Claude 订阅）。**深查 headless `claude -p`（B 方案）结论：此机不可行**——CLI 在（`claude.exe` v2.1.169，可被计划任务调用），正确的最小权限标志也确认存在（`--permission-mode dontAsk` 自动拒非白名单工具、`--allowedTools "Read(..)" "Write(..)"` 文件级限定、`--model sonnet`、`--max-budget-usd`、`--bare` 跳钩子、`-p` 配 `< /dev/null` 防 stdin 卡），机制能跑出 JSON——**但认证 401**：本机 Claude 认证是宿主/网关代理的（env 有 `ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL`+`CLAUDE_CODE_SDK_HAS_HOST_AUTH_REFRESH=1`），spawn 的无头进程拿不到该认证，单凭 `.credentials.json` 订阅 token 也没认证成（把网关/会话 env unset 后仍 401）。无人值守要可行须 `claude setup-token`（交互、仅用户能做）+ 落盘长期 token + 自主 agent——低频任务不划算。**故采用"会话内一键"**：新增 [`backfill_translations.py`](src/dashboard/backfill_translations.py)（`detect` 找缺口写 `_backfill_input.json` / `merge` 校验合并 `_backfill_output.json`→`translations.json` 并清理，确定性 Python）+ 斜杠命令 [`/backfill-translations`](.claude/commands/backfill-translations.md)（让当前会话的 Sonnet 跑完 detect→译→merge→重建）。**实测全流程**：删 `tech_rsi_14`→detect 找到 1→写译文→merge 还原→detect 报"无需补译"→重建后 🩺 翻译覆盖 185/185。零 key/token/无人值守 agent。副发现：无头会话结束会触发我的 SessionEnd 钩子，Windows 路径在 bash 下被打散（`--bare` 可规避）。*

*Update Note (2026-06-10, **看板自审源文件新鲜度/一致性（用户问"如何保障依赖文件随项目实时更新"）+ 因子表排序 + 会话去重 + 页面自动刷新**): 三批小迭代。**(1) 源文件新鲜度自审**——核心认知：看板只能忠实反映源文件、无法保证源文件自身新鲜（A类随治理 gate 自动更新如 registry/field_status/git/transcript；B类靠纪律如 project_state/FINDINGS/board.yaml；C类缓存如 translations.json）。解法是让看板**自检并标红落后**：新增 [`health.py`](src/dashboard/health.py) `collect_health`，落地页顶部"🩺 数据新鲜度/一致性自审"面板，每次重建跑 5 检查——① catalog（`catalog_composition()` 代码实时）vs registry 当前数（不一致→需 sync_catalog）② Sonnet 翻译覆盖缺口 ③ project_state 顶部 Update Note 日期 vs 最新 commit 日期（落后→补记录）④ 最近 `run_daily_qa` 通过率+时效（读 `logs/qa_report_*.json` 的 `checks[].ok`）⑤ 6 个关键源文件 mtime 一览。任一 warn→面板转琥珀。实测当前 3 ok+1 warn（QA 2 天前 8/10，正确暴露）。**(2) 因子表表头点击排序**（generic JS，整格判数值/字符串——`earn_..._60` 不误判为数字；OSAP/信号表同享）。**(3) 会话同标题去重**：67 transcript 里 0 真重复 id，但很多 session 同开场白（重发/续接）→ 按派生标题合并保留最近一条+`×N` 角标（67→29）。**(4) 页面自动刷新**：构建写根 `build_id.txt`（gitignore），页面每 30s 轮询比对烘焙的 `BUILD_ID`——后台/空闲标签页静默 reload、活动标签页弹"点击刷新"小条（实测空闲页自己 reload 成功）。全部 DOM eval 验证。构建 0.7s。*

*Update Note (2026-06-10, **看板 md 页内查看免手动：常驻本地服务（at-logon 计划任务）**): 用户不想每次手动双击 `serve_dashboard.bat`。解法：新增 **at-logon 计划任务 `QuantDashboardServe`** 用 pythonw 后台常驻一个绑 `127.0.0.1:8799` 的静默 http 服务，开机自动起 → 看板永远在 `http://127.0.0.1:8799/` 可用，md 页内查看一直生效，零手动。**踩了两个真坑**：(a) `Register-ScheduledTask` 的 `-AtLogOn` 默认全用户触发器→需管理员→"Access denied"；给触发器加 `-User <当前用户>` 限定即免提权。(b) **stock `python -m http.server` 在 pythonw（无窗口）下每个请求都返回空响应（HTTP 000）**——因为它把请求日志写 stderr，pythonw 没有 stderr 会抛错；故新增静默服务脚本 [`serve.py`](src/dashboard/serve.py)（`log_message` 置空 + `directory=ROOT`），pythonw 跑它 curl 实测 index/md 均 **HTTP 200**。NB 本机 venv 的 pythonw 是重定向器（会再 exec 基础 `C:\ProgramData\anaconda3\pythonw.exe`，双进程），任务直接用 anaconda pythonw（单进程、stdlib 足够）。新增 [`open_dashboard.bat`](src/dashboard/open_dashboard.bat)（一键开浏览器到该地址，或直接收藏 URL）；`serve_dashboard.bat` 降为手动备用。安全：仅 127.0.0.1，http.server 无 CORS 头→跨源读不到。三计划任务并存：`QuantDashboardRefresh`（每小时重建）+ `QuantDashboardServe`（常驻服务）+ SessionEnd 钩子（结束重建）。验证：任务 trigger=Logon、State=Running、serving HTTP 200。*

*Update Note (2026-06-09, **Part B (pit_* parity-validated vs vendor q_*) + Part C (3 PIT single-quarter margin factors added)** — follow-on to the indicators rebuild): **Part B** — validated our self-computed `pit_*` single-quarter YoY against Tushare's independent vendor `q_*` (recompute via the DEPLOYED `derive_single_quarter_value`+`percent_change`+`same_period_last_year_end` on the income ledger vs the raw indicators ledger's `q_netprofit_yoy`/`q_op_yoy`/`q_sales_yoy`; 253,692 firm-quarters). Result: **~90% near-exact** (|Δ|<0.05pp), Spearman 0.97-0.98, sign-agreement 99%, **Pearson 0.95-0.99 after clipping |YoY|>300%** — the raw Pearson near-0 (netprofit/sales) was PURELY ~1.5-3% extreme near-zero-base YoY blow-ups (our `percent_change` and the vendor clamp them differently; mathematical YoY-ratio instability, NOT a core-computation bug). **Verdict: our pit_* is correct/trustworthy** (growth factors should winsorize, as the library already does). Report [PIT_VS_VENDOR_Q_PARITY.md](workspace/research/data_audit/PIT_VS_VENDOR_Q_PARITY.md); script `workspace/scripts/validate_pit_vs_vendor_q.py` (pure pandas + deployed primitives, no qlib/loader/find/du). **Part C** — added 3 PIT single-quarter MARGIN factors to the catalog: `qual_q_net_margin` = `Ref($n_income_attr_p_sq_q0,1)/Ref($revenue_sq_q0,1)`, `qual_q_gross_margin` = `(Ref($revenue_sq_q0,1)-Ref($oper_cost_sq_q0,1))/Ref($revenue_sq_q0,1)`, `qual_q_op_margin` = `Ref($operate_profit_sq_q0,1)/Ref($revenue_sq_q0,1)` — the PIT-correct alternative to Tushare's vendor `q_netprofit_margin`/`q_gsprofit_margin`, built on the Part-B-validated single-quarter `_sq_q0` derivation. All fields field-approved (income `_sq` family); PIT-safe (every `$field` `Ref(...,1)`-wrapped). `catalog_composition().total` →185 (DERIVED, not pinned); synced to `factor_master` as **draft** (parity_ok, +3 rows). Tests: PIT-safety + `TestFormalFactorCompatibility` + `test_factor_registry` PASS. Expense-ratio / `*_to_ebt` single-quarter ratios DEFERRED (need `sell_exp_sq_q0`/`admin_exp_sq_q0`/`total_profit_sq_q0` approved first). These are `draft` factors — candidate/approved promotion is a separate gated step. Memory: [[project_field_parity_audit_2026_06_08]].*

*Update Note (2026-06-09, **EventDrivenBacktester 退市/停牌健壮性两处修复（用户指示）**): 修了 event-driven 引擎里两个与"停牌→NaN 价格"相关的健壮性缺陷。**(1) 策略下单 NaN 崩溃（原始任务）**：`RankedFallbackStrategy` 走的共享下单函数 [strategies.py `_emit_rebalance_orders`](src/backtest_engine/event_driven/strategies.py) 在 trim 分支用 `int(max(diff,0)/ref_price/lot)*lot`，当一个**持仓**当日停牌时 `prev_day` 收盘为 NaN → `ref_price=NaN`（`NaN<=0` 为 False，旧 `<=0` 守卫漏过）→ `int(NaN)` 抛 `ValueError: cannot convert float NaN to integer`，整个回测崩（topk=50 时一只分析师覆盖票中途停牌触发；topk=30 不触发）。修复：守卫改 `pd.isna(ref_price) or ref_price<=0` → 跳过 trim、把仓位结转到下次调仓（停牌票本就不可调；引擎另有 vol==0 代理在成交层 block）。买入分支无 `int()`、`max(NaN,…)`/`NaN>1.0` 不抛 → 已自然结转，不动。**(2) 退市 force-close 回退加固**：先用真实数据查清机制——退市与停牌由 **PIT universe 边界**（`all_stocks.txt`，`get_index_constituents('all')`→`D.list_instruments`）自然区分：停牌票仍在 universe → `D.features` 返回 **NaN 行**（实测 2023-06-15：5242 在册全部返回、0 缺行、57 只停牌票 vol/close/open 全 NaN）→ 在 `today_codes` 里 → **不 force-close、结转**；退市票退出 universe → 无行 → `_handle_delistings`（[engine.py](src/backtest_engine/event_driven/engine.py) `BacktestEngine` 方法，每交易日开盘前跑）force-close。**关键事实（决定不加 haircut）**：退市前的退市整理期暴跌**已逐日记在日线 `$close` 里**（实测 300280.SZ 峰值 6.99→最后成交 0.33 = −95%；000851.SZ 2.95→0.38 = −87%），持仓每日 MTM 跟着跌，最后在底部 force-close ⇒ 损失已建模，**再加 haircut 会重复计损** → 用户决定：不加 haircut，改加固第 4 层回退。两处软肋：旧逻辑只看 `prev_day` 一天，取不到真实价时退回 `avg_cost`（偏乐观），且若最后一根在册 bar 是 NaN 停牌行 → `shares*NaN` → 现金变 NaN。加固：引擎新增 `self._last_valid_price` **向前结转缓存**（在 `_record_day` 按真实(非 NaN、>0)收盘逐日更新，跨停牌缺口保留最后真实价）+ 新 `_resolve_delist_price()` 优先级 缓存→昨收(若真实)→`avg_cost`→`0.0`（绝不 NaN/负）；`Portfolio.force_close` 加 NaN/负价守卫（floor 到 0.0=全损，防 NaN 现金污染全簿）。退市数据来源已确认：`stock_basic.delist_date`（Tushare `list_status='L,D,P'`，每股精确退市日，319 只有值）+ `update_daily_data.py` 每日重抓覆盖 → 恢复数据更新后自动保鲜。测试：新增 [tests/backtest_engine/test_delisting_force_close.py](tests/backtest_engine/test_delisting_force_close.py)（13）+ `test_ranked_fallback_strategy.py` 新增 2（NaN 结转）；两处均经"临时回退证明测试能抓 bug"验证；**backtest_engine 全套 242 passed**。`force_close 永不产生 NaN/负现金` + `退市 force-close 用结转真实价、不加 haircut` 登记为 CLAUDE.md §3.3 不变量并镜像 AGENTS.md §2a.3。NOTE：workspace 原型 `event_driven_strategy_research.py` 的 `ScheduledLongOnlyStrategy` 仍带旧 NaN-trim 写法（研究脚本，未改）。*

*Update Note (2026-06-08f, **RULE CHANGE — leverage is NOT a viable option in strategy research (user directive); doc-only**): per user instruction, added a non-negotiable research rule: research/evaluate/report every strategy **unlevered** (gross ≤ 1× capital; no margin/borrowing past 100% invested), never propose leverage as a path to a return target, never headline a levered CAGR — the deployable number is the 1× number; long-only = fully-invested-or-cash, market-neutral = natural 1× (funded long/short). Rationale: leverage adds no edge, only multiplies vol+drawdown, and is self-defeating on a high-vol long-only book; deployment context assumes no leverage. Added to **CLAUDE.md §7 item 11**, **AGENTS.md §2a.3**, and **`.agents/rules/research-integrity.md` §8b** (mirrored same pass per §11.2). `config.yaml risk.max_leverage=1.5` left as a legacy field but flagged in the rule as NOT license to lever (not edited). NOTE this supersedes the leverage-frontier framing in the 2026-06-08 low-corr/MN research (`jq_replication/FINDINGS_lowcorr.md` + [[research_long_only_50cagr]]): the levered "~5× MN → ~50% CAGR" and "leveraged long-only" paths are now OUT OF SCOPE — the honest deployable ceiling is the 1× figure (long-only VQ10 ~+20.7%/−26.6%; unlevered low-corr MN Sharpe ~1.4-1.8 / CAGR ~12-15%). 50% CAGR is therefore NOT attainable in-scope.*

*Update Note (2026-06-04, **New hard invariant — price-return (vectorized) vs total-return (event-driven) added to `CLAUDE.md` §3.3 + §8.2 / `AGENTS.md` §2a.3; doc-only**): promoted the long_only finding (note further below) into a standing backtest-fidelity invariant after verifying the mechanism in code, not from the summary. `VectorizedBacktester` defaults to `deal_price='close'` and computes returns from the provider's RAW `$close` → PRICE return (a dividend/bonus ex-date drops price without crediting the distribution). `EventDrivenBacktester` credits post-tax cash dividends + bonus shares on the ex-date via [corporate_actions.py](src/backtest_engine/event_driven/corporate_actions.py) `CorporateActionHandler.process` (`cash_div_tax * shares` → `portfolio.credit_cash`; `stk_div * shares` → position) → TOTAL return. They diverge by ~the book's dividend yield: long_only value book EventDriven +11.64% vs vectorized +6.17% CAGR (2021-26); the phase6d monkeypatch that no-op'd `CorporateActionHandler.process` collapsed EventDriven to +6.59% ≈ vectorized = the isolating proof (dividends+bonus = +5.05% CAGR; not a leak/bug). Rule: never compare a vectorized price-return screen against an event-driven total-return run for a dividend-paying strategy without accounting for the gap; the event-driven total-return figure is the deployment number. Empirical finding, NO unit-test gate yet — candidate follow-up: a dividend-fixture regression pinning the `CorporateActionHandler.process` crediting + a vectorized-price-return-vs-event-total-return assertion. Doc-only; mirrored CLAUDE↔AGENTS in the same pass per §11.2.*

*Update Note (2026-06-04, **long_only PRIMARY EventDriven tradability check — TRADABLE @ +11.64% TOTAL return; vectorized=price-return vs EventDriven=total-return caveat; approved-factor strategy scoped; ebit deferred**): completed the FINDINGS.md-named un-run step for the `long_only_50cagr` defensive value+low-vol book — routed the FROZEN PRIMARY config (VL @ core, equal-weight top-40, monthly, RAW; the IS-tuned overlay was EXCLUDED — it failed OOS) through `EventDrivenBacktester` with realistic A-share frictions (`RankedFallbackStrategy` top-40-tradeable-of-120 + limit-up substitution, T+1, suspension, JoinQuant `CostConfig()` + default slippage, 10% ADV cap, benchmark CSI500). NOT fresh OOS — 2021-26 was already spent in phase5; this is an execution-realism re-check of the same frozen config (identical PIT-safe signal). **Result: +11.64% CAGR / −14.52% MDD / 0.80 Sharpe / 15.3% vol** over 2021-26, beating CSI500. **The EventDriven beat the phase5 vectorized OOS (+6.17%) — fully decomposed (§7.10, verified, NOT a leak/bug):** fill-timing ruled out (phase6b: vec open +6.13% ≈ close +6.17%); tradability filters ~0.7% (phase6c); **dividends DECISIVE (phase6d: EventDriven with `CorporateActionHandler.process` monkeypatched to no-op = +6.59% ≈ vectorized +6.17%) → cash-dividend + bonus-share crediting = +5.05% CAGR.** **PROJECT-WIDE BACKTEST CAVEAT (candidate for CLAUDE.md §8):** `VectorizedBacktester` with `deal_price='close'` (default) on this project's RAW-close provider reports **PRICE return** — it drops on ex-date WITHOUT crediting the dividend, understating a high-yield book by ~the dividend yield; `EventDrivenBacktester` reports **TOTAL return** (credits dividends+bonus on ex-date, PIT-correct). So **+11.64% total return is the correct deployment figure**; phase5 +6.17% was price-return-only. The book is a **deployable ~11–12% total-return / <15% MDD A-share strategy** — still NOT 50% CAGR (infeasible clean-PIT long-only, confirmed). Strategy-registry promotion remains gated by the promotion gate (not pursued). *Update Note (2026-06-02, **EventDrivenBacktester limit detection switched to Tushare stk_limit (primary) with computed-band fallback; stk_limit promoted quarantine→approved**): the event-driven engine previously ALWAYS recomputed limit-up/limit-down prices from `pre_close × regulatory band`. It now resolves through the new `Exchange.resolve_limit_prices()` ([src/backtest_engine/event_driven/exchange.py](src/backtest_engine/event_driven/exchange.py)), which **prefers Tushare's published `$up_limit` / `$down_limit`** (the exchange's own daily limit prices, already materialized as bare-name day bins) and **falls back to the computed round-half-up band** only when those fields are absent/NaN. `is_limit_up` / `is_limit_down` now detect against the resolved prices (so `strategies.RankedFallbackStrategy` and `can_buy` / `can_sell` inherit it). `$up_limit` / `$down_limit` were added to `ENGINE_REQUIRED_FIELDS` ([constants.py](src/backtest_engine/event_driven/constants.py)) so formal runs preload them and never fall into per-day `D.features`; `_fetch_day_data` now derives its fetch list from `ENGINE_REQUIRED_FIELDS` (single source of truth) and renames the two columns. **Why Tushare-primary:** the published values carry the exact fen-rounding, the ex-rights adjustment, and special regimes the band formula misses (the pre-2023 main-board IPO-first-day +44%/−36% asymmetric rule; and post-2023 registration-system IPO no-limit windows encoded as a wide sentinel up_limit≈1e6 / down_limit≈0.01). **Why a fallback is still needed (empirically verified, not assumed):** [workspace/scripts/diag_stk_limit_coverage.py](workspace/scripts/diag_stk_limit_coverage.py) scanned traded stock-days (vol>0, real stocks only, indices excluded) across 2014/2018/2021/2024/2026 — **2024+ has zero holes**, but pre-2022 has small explained holes (2021 = 2.17%, dominated by Beijing-Stock-Exchange names during the 2021 launch where Tushare had no `stk_limit` row yet; plus IPO no-limit days and a few legacy main-board names). Value sanity: ≥99.79% of present rows land on a regulatory tier (±5/10/20/30%) (worst window 2021 = 99.7957%; 2024/2026 ≈ 99.94/99.96%); the residual is no-limit sentinel rows (registration-system IPO no-limit days, counted off-tier because their implied band is ~thousands of %), the pre-2023 main-board IPO first-day +44%/−36% rule, and penny-stock fen-rounding — all correct. **Governance (user-approved full promotion):** `stk_limit` moved `quarantine → approved` in [config/field_registry/field_status.yaml](config/field_registry/field_status.yaml) with a bound approval YAML ([config/field_registry/approvals/2026-06-02_stk_limit_quarantine_to_approved.yaml](config/field_registry/approvals/2026-06-02_stk_limit_quarantine_to_approved.yaml), bound to `provider_build_id=prod_full_20260421_namespace_v1` / `calendar_policy_id=frozen_20260227_system_build`) + an append-only [field_approval_log.jsonl](config/field_registry/field_approval_log.jsonl) entry. These are execution fields knowable at session open (pre-determined from the prior close), so no `Ref` lag is required. **Tests:** new `tests/backtest_engine/test_exchange_limits.py::ResolveLimitPricesTests` (primary-beats-computed, IPO-44% case, fallback-on-absent/NaN); `tests/data_infra/test_field_registry.py::TestLiveRegistry::test_stk_limit_bare_fields_approved_for_formal` (flipped from the old quarantine assertion). Sweep: 68 (exchange-limits + field-registry) + 125 (preload-hardening + approval-evidence + field-dependency-gate + PR9 compat) + 11 (event-driven wiring + dormant-module boundaries) all green; both lints (`no_bare_qlib_features`, `unsafe_pit_dates`) clean; end-to-end smoke confirms the fields preload and the exchange detects limits via them. Docs synced: CLAUDE.md §3 (new invariant + PR5 seed line + PR9a guardrail line), AGENTS.md (mirror), [src/backtest_engine/README.md](src/backtest_engine/README.md), [data/data_dictionary.md](data/data_dictionary.md). No on-disk / pipeline change — the bins already existed; the engine now consumes what it had materialized. **Verified no-limit-day behavior:** Tushare encodes genuinely-no-limit stock-days (ChiNext/STAR/post-2023 main-board first 5 days; BSE listing day) as a WIDE SENTINEL (`up_limit≈1e5/1e6`, `down_limit≈0.01/0.00`), NOT NaN — so the primary path correctly treats them as freely tradable (close never within 0.005 of the sentinel); true non-stock instruments (indices) are the only NaN rows. Evidence: [workspace/scripts/diag_stk_limit_nolimit_days.py](workspace/scripts/diag_stk_limit_nolimit_days.py); pinned by `test_no_limit_day_sentinel_is_not_a_limit` / `test_no_limit_day_bse_sentinel`. **KNOWN FOLLOW-UP (deferred to a future task, chip spawned 2026-06-02):** in OLDER provider data (pre-~2022; e.g. the ~6952 IPO-window NaN rows seen in 2018) some no-limit IPO days were published as NaN rather than the sentinel, so they hit the computed-band fallback; `can_buy` is protected by `is_ipo_period()` but `can_sell` has no IPO override, so a no-limit IPO day that closes exactly on the spurious computed `limit_down` could be wrongly blocked from selling. Rare, pre-2022 only, NOT a regression (the prior computed-only code behaved identically). Candidate fix: add an `is_ipo_period()` short-circuit to `can_sell` (symmetric with `can_buy`) and/or have `resolve_limit_prices` return a no-limit sentinel when `is_ipo_period()` is True, with a regression test in [tests/backtest_engine/test_exchange_limits.py](tests/backtest_engine/test_exchange_limits.py).*

same MultiIndex-order class as the Phase-6 `build_is_windowed_panel` bug). **Fix:** a shared name-based `_date_level_key` resolver (prefer the `datetime`-named level; dtype fallback; **fail-closed** — NO positional-0 fallback, that IS the leak path) used by all 4 helpers; Inverse predictors aren't read as long-only-positive (evidence also stores the signed `is_rank_icir`). **Tests:** [test_cross_sectional_helpers.py](tests/alpha_research/test_cross_sectional_helpers.py) (10: order-invariance for all 4, the no-future-dependence leak test PROVEN to fail pre-fix, zero-std NaN, fail-closed) + Layer-2 builder tests in [test_factor_lifecycle_walk_forward.py](tests/alpha_research/test_factor_lifecycle_walk_forward.py) (dependency-exclusion, belt, base-only equivalence, wrong-order fail-closed, expected_direction) + dataset_build base/composite/industry split + unknown-raises in [test_factor_lifecycle_steps.py](tests/research_orchestrator/test_factor_lifecycle_steps.py). Committed `c91cda9` (build) + must-fix + enum-validation; re-confirm = **GO**. **MERGED** PR [#36](https://github.com/henrydan111/quant-system/pull/36) (`c587e44`) → `wave1-field-promotion`. **OPERATIONAL RUN COMPLETE (2026-06-02):** dry-run (15 candidate + 1 IS-draft) → temp-registry orchestrator validation (all 3 Layer-2 paths incl. `mom_idio_20d` size-neutralize+market_cap) → live (parity-clean, no sync). **15 promoted draft→candidate** (11 composites + 4 industry-rel); `comp_momentum_quality` stayed DRAFT (full-window OOS-stable but IS sign-consistency 0.571<0.70 — the gate filtering, not OOS data). **Live registry now 87 candidate + 84 draft** (72 base Phase 6 + 15 Layer-2 Phase 7); `expected_direction` persisted (3 inverse: `mom_idio_20d`/`mom_industry_rel_20d`/`comp_52w_position`); 87 lifecycle evidence rows (oos all-NA, no approved). `oos_informed_backfill` funnel (24→16→15) + caveats in [phase7_selection_provenance.json](workspace/research/factor_expansion/phase7_selection_provenance.json) + a `testing_ledger` `phase7_selection_funnel` event (2021-2026 burned; candidate≠approved). **Factor-lifecycle arc (Phases 1-7) COMPLETE — 87 of 171 catalog factors `candidate`.** The 6 sealed-OOS expansion winners remain their SEPARATE governed sealed-OOS/promotion path. WIP still stashed at `stash@{0}`. Non-blocking future cleanup (GPT): `operators.neutralize` has positional assumptions but Phase 7 uses `factor_eval.neutralization.neutralize_size_industry` which already normalizes the index.*

*Update Note (2026-06-01, **Factor-lifecycle formalization PHASE 6 COMPLETE — first operational `factor_lifecycle` run; 72 base factors promoted draft→candidate on the LIVE registry** (branch `factor-lifecycle-p6`)): ran the Phase-5 IS-only gate on the **147 base catalog factors** end-to-end through the orchestrator. **Result: 72 promoted to `status=candidate`** (+ 72 definition-bound FORMAL evidence rows, `formal_evidence_eligible=True`, `oos_rank_icir`=NA [no OOS leak], NEVER `approved`); live registry now **72 candidate + 99 draft** (171 current). **Pipeline:** 147 base → 114 field-eligible (33 quarantine/pending `$field` auto-excluded: alpha_*/flow_*/margin_*/north_*) → 85 IS-candidates (|heldout rank_icir|≥0.10 ∧ yearly sign-consistency≥0.70) → **72 promoted = the OOS-stable subset** (the 13 IS-candidates whose INDEPENDENT full-window 2014-2026 evidence collapses/flips OOS were EXCLUDED from the consumed batch; 8 of those 13 are the `grow_*`/`earn_earnings_momentum` earnings-LEVEL factors already known IS-overfit). User chose "promote 72 OOS-stable only" (vs all 85) after the clarification that **`candidate` is an ADDITIVE tier — it does NOT restrict research use** (`get_factor_catalog()` stays authoritative for ALL discovery/sandbox; the registry status gates only FORMAL hypothesis_validation components, and `candidate` can never auto-become `approved` — that needs the separate P1.1 OOS/promotion gate). **GPT-mandated safety arc honored:** compute-only dry-run ([phase6_factor_lifecycle_dry_run.py](workspace/scripts/phase6_factor_lifecycle_dry_run.py), cross-checked vs the prior catalog-revalidation CSV — IS ICIR reproduces) → temp-registry orchestrator validation (3-factor end-to-end) → live sync → live 72-run. **TWO real merged-code bugs found by the operational run + fixed (each with a regression test proven to fail pre-fix):** (1) **Phase-4 MultiIndex level-order** — [build_is_windowed_panel](src/alpha_research/factor_lifecycle/walk_forward_validation.py) hardcoded an `(instrument,datetime)` future-price index, but `compute_factors` returns `(datetime,instrument)`; the POSITIONAL `adj.reindex` matched NOTHING → all-NaN label → empty-panel `IsEndLeakageError`. The Phase-4 fixtures only ever used `(instrument,datetime)` so the integration point was untested. Fixed: build the future index in the panel's actual level order (robust to either) + a loud guard if current prices match but all future prices are NaN. Regression: `test_build_is_multiindex_level_order_invariant`. (2) **Phase-5 publish resume-safety** — [factor_lifecycle_registry_publish](src/research_orchestrator/factor_lifecycle_steps.py) read verdicts from the in-memory `context.state["factor_lifecycle"]`, but the gate pauses split the run across processes and `reconstruct_state_from_completed_steps` restores ONLY `step_outputs` on resume → on a real (paused) run it would promote NOTHING. Fixed: read verdicts from the PERSISTED `factor_lifecycle_walk_forward` step_outputs (in-memory fallback for the no-pause path). Regression: `test_publish_reads_verdicts_from_persisted_step_outputs_on_resume`. **1-factor benign sync:** `rev_up_down_ratio_20d` re-versioned to v3 (catalog refactored `Count(…>0,20)/20`→equivalent `Sum(If(…>0,1,0),20)/20`; same factor, drifted hash) via `sync_catalog_to_registry` so the resolver P1.3 gate passed (it's in the 72). **Run mechanics for reuse:** factor_lifecycle is formal-only → needs a Hypothesis (no floor rails apply — not in `SUCCESS_CRITERIA_FLOORS`); success_criteria sets ONLY `min_rank_icir` (others None → no null hard rules → automated verdict honestly "accepted"); the 2 gate pauses are driven by [phase6_drive_gates.py](workspace/scripts/phase6_drive_gates.py) (concern scores keyed to `min_rank_icir`, then `gate_decision=approved`); request built by [phase6_setup_request.py](workspace/scripts/phase6_setup_request.py). Tests: factor_lifecycle+registry suite 81 passed. **NOT done / follow-ups:** the **24 composite + industry-relative** factors (Layer-2 `add_composites` gating); the **6 sealed-OOS expansion winners** still take their SEPARATE governed sealed-OOS / promotion path (register definitions first); the user's OOS-fix **WIP is still STASHED** at `stash@{0}` (restore via `git stash pop` — disjoint from this work). **Committed `38ba203` on `factor-lifecycle-p6`; PR [#35](https://github.com/henrydan111/quant-system/pull/35) → `wave1-field-promotion`.** **GPT PR-#35 cross-review = GO to merge** (both fixes confirmed correct + complete, no code-level leakage hole, 57 focused tests pass, live-registry probe matches: 72 candidate / 99 draft / 0 approved, 72 definition-bound formal_evidence_eligible rows, no non-null OOS metric) **with one governance follow-up (resolved, not a merge blocker):** the 72 are an **`oos_informed_backfill`** — the IS-only validator was NOT contaminated (OOS never entered labels/folds/metrics/set_status; evidence rows are IS-only), but the SELECTION of which factors became candidate used pre-existing full-window OOS knowledge to exclude the 13 collapsers, so **the 72 must NEVER be described later as a fresh OOS-free selection**, and **2021-2026 is ALREADY BURNED for these 72** (a future candidate→approved promotion MUST use a genuinely-sealed window, not 2021-2026). Resolved by recording the FULL selection funnel (147 base → 114 field-eligible → 85 IS-candidates → 72 promoted, 13 excluded, 33 field-ineligible) + the `oos_informed_backfill` label in a committed artifact [workspace/research/factor_expansion/phase6_selection_provenance.json](workspace/research/factor_expansion/phase6_selection_provenance.json) AND a live `testing_ledger` `factor_lifecycle:phase6_selection_funnel` event (the prior `batch_effective_trials=72` was accurate for the consumed run but incomplete for the full multiple-testing surface).*

*Update Note (2026-06-01, **Factor-lifecycle formalization PHASE 5 MERGED — orchestrator `factor_lifecycle` profile (the IS-only draft→candidate factor gate) to `wave1-field-promotion`** (PR [#34](https://github.com/henrydan111/quant-system/pull/34), merge commit `cddc7bd`)): a NEW formal orchestrator profile (the **8th** built-in) wires the merged IS-only walk-forward validator (`run_is_walk_forward`) into the DAG as the `draft→candidate` factor gate. **IS-ONLY by construction (orchestrator-level mirror of the Phase-4 leakage guard):** the compiled DAG has NO `oos_test` stage, NO event/vectorized OOS backtest, NO holdout-seal claim (the seal only fires on `oos_test`); the `candidate→approved` OOS spend is a SEPARATE frozen-set/promotion-gate path. 6 slices, each committed + tested: (1) profile + `_factor_lifecycle_dag_builder` ([engine.py](src/research_orchestrator/engine.py)) + `walk_forward_validation` capability; (2) `factor_lifecycle_object_resolver` (DRAFT-accepting allow-set; reuses P1.3 `_assert_no_definition_drift` + PER-FACTOR field gate via `evaluate_field_dependencies`); (3) `factor_lifecycle_dataset_build` (IS-only `load_is_windowed_panel` for field-eligible base factors only; disallowed `$field` never reaches compute; composites deferred); (4) `factor_lifecycle_walk_forward` (`run_is_walk_forward` → candidate/draft verdicts, no `oos_*`, + per-factor & batch-effective-trials events to the file-locked `TestingLedgerStore`; `factor_origin∈{generated,a_priori}` fail-closed); (5) gate-metrics branch in `_collect_measured_values` (maps max `|heldout ICIR|`→`rank_icir` so `criteria_results` is non-empty); (6) `factor_lifecycle_registry_publish` (DIRECT decision matrix, NOT `_assert_gate_allows_publication`: only human `approved` writes a FORMAL idempotent lifecycle evidence row [`store.record_lifecycle_evidence`, `formal_evidence_eligible=True`, definition-bound, no `oos_*`] THEN `set_status('candidate')` non-privileged; rejected/quarantined/missing → no writes; NEVER `approved`). Handlers in [src/research_orchestrator/factor_lifecycle_steps.py](src/research_orchestrator/factor_lifecycle_steps.py). **Design arc:** spec → conditional-GO ×2 (4 must-fixes: new draft-accepting resolver, direct publish matrix, gate-metrics non-empty, per-factor field exclusion) → GO; slice-1 separately GPT-GO'd (folded forward guidance: evidence idempotency, runtime no-seal guard, criteria_results non-empty). **WIP NOTE:** the user's `engine.py`/`validation_steps.py` OOS-fix WIP collided with the Phase-5 `engine.py` edits; per the user's call it was STASHED (`stash@{0}` "user-wip-oos-vacuous-trade-fix") so Phase 5 builds clean — restore via `git stash pop` (disjoint function from the factor_lifecycle additions; applies cleanly). **GPT PR-#34 post-impl review (NO-GO → 4 fixes → GO + MERGED):** (1) `record_lifecycle_evidence` independently fail-closes on definition drift (skipped_drift/skipped_unknown); (2) maps `n_heldout_blocks`→`selected_fold_count`; (3) profile `consumes_types` narrowed to `("factor",)` (composite gating a follow-up); (4) publish emits `produced_objects` (promoted factors at status `candidate`) for lineage. **Tests:** [test_factor_lifecycle_{profile,steps}.py](tests/research_orchestrator/) = 17; regression sweep 237 (registry+orchestrator) passed / the 1 pre-existing wave1 failure (`test_event_orchestrator` `_fake_backtest_stage` stale mock — NOT mine, NOT the WIP, proven isolated) is outside that sweep. With the WIP stashed the previously-WIP-caused OOS-handler test now passes. **WIP:** still stashed at `stash@{0}` ("user-wip-oos-vacuous-trade-fix") — restore via `git stash pop` (disjoint from the factor_lifecycle additions; applies cleanly). **NOT done:** no actual run (Phase 6 runs the profile on the 171 + 6 OOS candidates); composite/industry-relative gating (add_composites in dataset_build) is a follow-up. **Integration cross-review (GPT, pre-Phase-6, 2026-06-01) = GO:** a holistic review of the merged Phases 1-5 found NO cross-phase code must-fix (55 tests pass) — the leakage guarantee holds end-to-end (Phase-5 no-`oos_test`/no-seal DAG → Phase-4 `is_end`-bounded `load_is_windowed_panel`), the `candidate→approved` boundary is intact (Phase 5 only writes non-privileged `candidate`; `formal_evidence_eligible=True` lifecycle evidence is NOT read by the promotion gate — registry evidence, not promotion proof), and cross-phase reuse (P1.3 drift, evidence schema, `formal_validation` field gate) is consistent. **NEXT = Phase 6 (operational run; REFINED per the review — the earlier "gated 171/6 backfill" framing was imprecise):** run `factor_lifecycle` on the **147 BASE factors ONLY** (probe: 114 field-eligible, 33 field-ineligible → auto-excluded), NOT all 171; the **24 composite + industry-relative** factors are DEFERRED (Layer-2 `add_composites` compute is the follow-up; profile `consumes_types=("factor",)`). *Update Note (2026-06-01, **Factor-lifecycle formalization PHASE 4 MERGED — walk-forward revalidation modules to `wave1-field-promotion`** (PR [#33](https://github.com/henrydan111/quant-system/pull/33), merge commit `b47432c`)): the legacy walk-forward revalidation scripts are ported into a tested package [src/alpha_research/factor_lifecycle/](src/alpha_research/factor_lifecycle/) (`metrics`/`status_rules`/`revalidation`/`walk_forward_validation`/`report`). **TWO strictly-separated modes (the separation IS the leakage guard):** (1) **`run_is_walk_forward`** (FORMAL, IS-only, `draft→candidate`) is structurally bounded to `TimeSplit.is_end`. Design review caught that the forward-return label is FUTURE-looking (`Ref(ADJ_CLOSE, 0 - h)`) so bounding the factor date alone leaks — THREE belts enforce the label-realization boundary: `horizons=None` compute over `[is_start, is_end]`; label from adj-close capped at `is_end` (`shift(-h)` drops the last `h` rows); `IsWindowedPanel` raises `IsEndLeakageError` unless `max_factor_date` AND `max_label_realization_date` (`+h` TRADING days via `trade_cal.parquet`) are `≤ is_end`. IS-internal holdout = 3+1+1 (default 5+2+1 → 0 folds for 2014-2020); generated factor with no heldout RAISES (fail-closed); NO `oos_*` field; `evidence_kind` on result + each row. (2) **`run_historical_*`** (NON-formal full-window IS+OOS) = faithful port labeled `historical_investigation`; `revalidate_*.py` → thin wrappers. Split status rules (`assign_historical_status` oos-based vs `assign_candidate_status` IS-only); long-only viability stays Phase-2 metadata. **Design arc:** spec → conditional-GO (3 must-fixes: label-realization boundary, 3+1+1 fold config, split status rules) → re-confirm GO (IS-internal holdout config, evidence_kind first-class, trading-day `t+h`). **Tests:** [test_factor_lifecycle_{metrics,revalidation,walk_forward}.py](tests/alpha_research/) = 34 (label-realization leakage bound, 0-fold pin, fail-closed, spy `horizons=None`, no-`oos_*`, metric parity, CSV round-trip through Phase-2 import, + the GPT P0/P1 regression tests); regression sweep 49 (architecture + factor_lifecycle) green; PIT002 lint clean for the new code. **GPT PR-#33 post-impl review (NO-GO → 2 fixes → GO):** (P0) `build_is_windowed_panel`'s `shift(-h)`-over-rows could use a later adj-close row past `is_end` for a sparse/uncapped series (REPRODUCED — label used the OOS price) — fixed by the exact-calendar `r(t)` lookup + belt-0 input caps + index-alignment assertion; (P1) unknown `factor_origin` silently took `a_priori` — now raises. **Scope/NOT done:** modules + tests + thin wrappers only — NO new revalidation RUN (existing CSVs stand); the formal candidate gate is not yet orchestrator-wired (Phase 5). **Standing:** the 2 long-standing WIP-caused test failures (`engine.py`/`validation_steps.py`) persist, proven unrelated. **NEXT = Phase 5:** orchestrator `factor_lifecycle` profile (wires `run_is_walk_forward` into the discovery→candidate flow), then Phase 6 gated 171/6 backfill.*
